  <description
               value="A broad cancer-related value set containing both primary and secondary tumor types, with codes from ICD-10 and SNOMED CT, including both diagnosis and histology/morphology/behavior codes. ICD-O-3 morphology codes may also be used and are considered conformant to the specification. For SNOMED, the value set includes all codes descending from 363346000 &#39;Malignant neoplastic disease (disorder)&#39; and 108369006 &#39;Neoplasm (morphologic abnormality)&#39;."/>
